<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:24.5pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On
August&nbsp;25, 2004, Coldwater Creek Inc. issued a press release announcing
its financial results for its fiscal quarter ended July&nbsp;31, 2004. A copy
of the press release is set forth as Exhibit 99.1.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:24.5pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

information being furnished in this Item 2.02 and in Exhibit 99.1 shall not be
deemed &#147;filed&#148; for purposes of Section&nbsp;18 of the Securities Exchange Act
of 1934, as amended (the &#147;Exchange Act&#148;), or incorporated by reference in any
filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended or the Exchange Act,
whether made before or after the date of this report, except as shall be
expressly set forth by specific reference in such filing.</font></p>

  <p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;">&nbsp;</p>
  </td>
 </tr>

  <td width="54%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:54.58%;">

  Dennis Pence</font></p>

<head>





</head>

<body lang="EN-US" link="blue" vlink="purple">

<div>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit 99.1</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Coldwater Creek Announces Fiscal 2004 Second
Quarter Results</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Sandpoint, Idaho, August&nbsp;25, 2004 &#150; Coldwater Creek Inc. (Nasdaq:
CWTR) today reported financial results for the three- and six-month periods
ended July&nbsp;31, 2004. All per share amounts below reflect a 50 percent
stock dividend having the effect of a 3-for-2 stock split declared by the
company&#146;s board of directors on June&nbsp;14, 2004, and the company&#146;s
previously announced May 2004 public stock offering.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Consolidated Results</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the three-month period ended July&nbsp;31, 2004, net income was
$3.4 million, or $0.08 per diluted share, compared with a net loss of $1.4
million, or $0.04 loss per share, for the three-month period ended
August&nbsp;2, 2003.&#160; Net sales in the
fiscal 2004 second quarter increased 15.1 percent to $111.2 million from $96.7
million in the fiscal 2003 second quarter.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the six-month period ended July&nbsp;31, 2004, net income was $8.9
million, or $0.23 per diluted share, compared with net income of $0.5 million,
or $0.01 per diluted share, for the six-month period ended August&nbsp;2,
2003.&#160; Net sales in the first six months
of fiscal 2004 increased 11.2 percent to $235.7 million from $211.9 million in
the same period last year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;The improved net sales and net income results for the second quarter
were primarily due to continued strong customer response to our merchandise,&#148;
said Dennis Pence, chairman and chief executive officer.&#160; &#147;We were especially pleased with the ongoing
positive performance of our retail stores, which grew to represent half of the
company&#146;s total business for the first six months of the fiscal year.&#160; Based on these results, we now plan to open a
total of 49 stores in fiscal 2004, which will give us 115 locations across the
country at the start of the holiday season.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;Strong full-price selling in our spring and summer assortments across
all channels delivered higher merchandise margins and helped generate a
640-basis-point improvement in our gross profit rate,&#148; said Georgia
Shonk-Simmons, president and chief merchandising officer.&#160; &#147;Additionally, we are entering the fall
selling season with a very clean and current inventory position.&#160; At the same time, higher response rates to
our catalog mailings resulting from our focused catalog circulation strategy
contributed to a 70-basis-point decrease in selling, general and administrative
expenses expressed as a percentage of net sales.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Gross profit for the fiscal 2004 second quarter was $46.9 million, or
42.2 percent of net sales, compared with $34.7 million, or 35.8 percent of net
sales, for the fiscal 2003 second quarter.&#160;
The increase in gross profit dollars and rate was primarily attributable
to improved merchandise margins on sales in all channels, reduced clearance
activity and improved leveraging of the company&#146;s full-line retail store
occupancy costs.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Selling, general and administrative expenses for the fiscal 2004 second
quarter were $41.5 million, or 37.3 percent of net sales, compared with $36.8
million, or 38.0 percent of net sales, for the fiscal 2003 second quarter.&#160; Selling, general and administrative expenses
expressed as a percentage of net sales decreased primarily due to improved
response rates to catalogs mailed during the period partially offset by
increased employee expenses, primarily associated with the company&#146;s retail
expansion.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>


<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\jpatrow\04-9944-1\task177430\9944-1-mm.htm',USER='jpatrow',CD='Aug 25 12:52 2004' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Income from operations for the fiscal 2004 second quarter was $5.4
million, or 4.9 percent of net sales, compared with a loss from operations of
$2.1 million, or a negative 2.2 percent of net sales, for the fiscal 2003
second quarter.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Retail Segment Sales</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net sales from the Retail Segment, which includes the company&#146;s
full-line retail stores, resort stores and outlet stores, increased 51.0
percent to $61.3 million in the fiscal 2004 second quarter, from $40.6 million
in the fiscal 2003 second quarter.&#160;
Retail Segment net sales represented 55.1 percent of the company&#146;s total
net sales in the fiscal 2004 second quarter, compared with 42.0 percent in the
fiscal 2003 second quarter.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net sales from the Retail Segment increased 59.4 percent to $117.8
million in the first six months of fiscal 2004, from $73.9 million in the first
six months of fiscal 2003.&#160; Retail
Segment net sales represented 50.0 percent of the company&#146;s total net sales in
the first six months of fiscal 2004, compared with 34.9 percent in the
comparable prior year period.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The company opened 18 full-line retail stores during the fiscal 2004
second quarter for a total of 89 full-line retail stores in operation at the
end of the fiscal 2004 second quarter, compared with 48 full-line retail stores
at the end of the fiscal 2003 second quarter.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Direct Segment Sales</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;In keeping with our strategic shift toward a retail store-based
business model, we reduced catalog circulation by 32.3 percent in the second
quarter, and catalog net sales fell 26.0 percent compared with the prior year,&#148;
Pence said.&#160; &#147;Meanwhile, our e-commerce
net sales climbed by 9.8 percent during the period, due to effective e-mail
promotions.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net sales from the Direct Segment, which encompasses the company&#146;s
catalog and e-commerce businesses, decreased 10.9 percent to $49.9 million in
the fiscal 2004 second quarter from $56.1 million in the fiscal 2003 second
quarter.&#160; Direct Segment net sales
represented 44.9 percent of the company&#146;s total net sales in the fiscal 2004
second quarter, compared with 58.0 percent in the fiscal 2003 second quarter.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net sales from the Direct Segment decreased 14.5 percent to $117.9
million in the first six months of fiscal 2004 from $138.0 million in the same
period a year ago.&#160; Direct Segment net
sales represented 50.0 percent of the company&#146;s total net sales in the first
six months of fiscal 2004, compared with 65.1 percent in the comparable period
last year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Catalog Sales</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Catalog net sales decreased 26.0 percent to $24.0 million in the fiscal
2004 second quarter from $32.4 million in the fiscal 2003 second quarter.&#160; Catalog net sales represented 48.0 percent of
the Direct Segment&#146;s net sales in the fiscal 2004 second quarter, compared with
57.8 percent in the fiscal 2003 second quarter.&#160;
Catalog net sales represented 21.6 percent of the company&#146;s total net
sales in the fiscal 2004 second quarter, compared with 33.6 percent in the
fiscal 2003 second quarter.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>


<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\jpatrow\04-9944-1\task177430\9944-1-mm.htm',USER='jpatrow',CD='Aug 25 12:52 2004' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Catalog net sales decreased 27.3 percent to $57.0 million in the first
six months of fiscal 2004 from $78.4 million in the same period last year.&#160; Catalog net sales represented 48.4 percent of
the Direct Segment&#146;s net sales in the first six months of fiscal 2004, compared
with 56.8 percent in the comparable period a year ago.&#160; Catalog net sales represented 24.2 percent of
the company&#146;s total net sales in the first six months of fiscal 2004, compared
with 37.0 percent in the same period last year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">E-commerce Sales</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">E-commerce net sales increased 9.8 percent to $26.0 million in the
fiscal 2004 second quarter from $23.6 million in the fiscal 2003 second
quarter.&#160; E-commerce net sales
represented 52.0 percent of the Direct Segment&#146;s net sales in the fiscal 2004
second quarter, compared with 42.2 percent in the fiscal 2003 second
quarter.&#160; E-commerce net sales
represented 23.3 percent of the company&#146;s total net sales in the fiscal 2004
second quarter, compared with 24.5 percent in the fiscal 2003 second quarter.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">E-commerce net sales increased 2.2 percent to $60.9 million in the
first six months of fiscal 2004 from $59.6 million in the same period last
year.&#160; E-commerce net sales represented
51.6 percent of the Direct Segment&#146;s net sales in the first six months of
fiscal 2004, compared with 43.2 percent in the comparable period a year
ago.&#160; E-commerce net sales represented
25.8 percent of the company&#146;s total net sales in the first six months of fiscal
2004, compared with 28.1 percent in the same period last year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Liquidity</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">At the end of the fiscal 2004 first quarter, the company had no short
or long-term debt and a cash position of $88.6 million compared with a cash
position of $3.5 million at the end of the fiscal 2003 second quarter.&#160; The company&#146;s working capital increased to
$101.9 million at the end of the fiscal 2004 second quarter from $37.3 million
at the end the fiscal 2003 second quarter.&#160;
These results include net proceeds of $42.1 million from the company&#146;s
recent stock offering.&#160; Inventory
decreased $10.2 million, or 15.1 percent, to $57.4 million at the end of the
fiscal 2004 second quarter from $67.6 million at the end of the fiscal 2003
second quarter.&#160; This decrease occurred
at the same time the company added 41 full-line retail stores since the end of
the fiscal 2003 second quarter.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As previously announced,
Coldwater Creek will host a conference call on Wednesday, August&nbsp;25, 2004
at 4:45 p.m. (Eastern) to discuss fiscal 2004 second quarter results.&#160; To listen to the live Web cast, log on to
http://phx.corporate-ir.net/playerlink.zhtml?c=92631&amp;s=wm&amp;e=925613.
Also, a link to the live Web cast of the call is provided in the company&#146;s Web
site at www.coldwatercreek.com.&#160; The call
will be archived from approximately one hour after the conference call until
midnight on Wednesday, September&nbsp;1, 2004.&#160;
The replay can be accessed by dialing (719) 457-0820 and giving the
passcode &#147;601031&#148;.&#160; Any additional
information provided during the call will be available by accessing the replay
of the call.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Coldwater Creek is an integrated multi-sales channel retailer of
women&#146;s apparel, jewelry, footwear, gift items and accessories through a
growing number of full-line retail stores located in major metropolitan areas,
an e-commerce web site at www.coldwatercreek.com and direct-mail catalogs.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">This news release contains &#147;forward-looking statements&#148; within the

initiatives, marketing costs, realized and anticipated cost-efficiencies,
selling, general and administrative expenses, retail expansion, sales and
revenue growth, and financial performance.&#160;
These statements are based on management&#146;s current expectations and are
subject to a number of uncertainties and risks.&#160;
Actual results may differ materially.&#160;
Important factors that could cause actual results to differ materially
from estimates or projections contained in the forward-looking statements
include, but are not limited to, our inability to realize the full value of
merchandise currently in inventory as a result of sluggish sales, ever-changing
customer tastes and buying trends, and the current economic climate, which
continues to adversely affect the retail sector; unanticipated increases in
mailing and printing costs; the cost of additional overhead that may be
required to expand our brand; the possibility that our buy now/wear now
strategy will not be appealing to customers, and that it could be impacted by
unseasonable weather patterns, the difficult selling environment or other
factors beyond our control; unexpected or increased costs or delays in the
development and expansion of our retail chain and our potential inability to
recover these costs due to sluggish sales; the inherent difficulty in
forecasting consumer buying patterns and trends, particularly in the current
difficult economic climate and the possibility that any recent improvements in
our product margins, or in customer response to our merchandise, may not be
sustained; our inability to continue to fund our retail expansion with
operating cash as a result of either lower sales or higher than anticipated
costs, or both; uncertainties related to our shift to a triple-channel model,
in particular, the effects of shifting patterns of e-commerce or retail
purchases versus catalog purchases; and such other factors as are discussed in
our Form 10-Q Quarterly Reports and in our most recent Form 10-K Annual Report
filed with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission (&#147;SEC&#148;).&#160; We believe that these forward-looking
statements are reasonable; however, you should not place undue reliance on

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.6in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note (a):</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>For
the three-month period ended August&nbsp;2, 2003, 398 thousand potentially
dilutive common shares were excluded from average shares because they were
antidilutive.&#160; These potentially dilutive
common shares were anitdilutive because the Company reported a net loss in the
three-month period ended August&nbsp;2, 2003.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt -.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .6in;text-indent:-.6in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note (b):</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
above weighted average shares outstanding and net income (loss) per share
amounts reflect three 50% stock dividends each having the effect of a 3-for-2
stock split declared by the Board of Directors on December&nbsp;19, 2002,
August&nbsp;4, 2003 and June&nbsp;14, 2004.</p>
